    def test_priority_chain(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        """Source priority order."""
        value_file = write_text(tmp_path / "port.txt", "  42  \n")
        schema_path = _write_schema(
            tmp_path,
            {
                "host": {
                    "type": "string",
                    "default": "localhost",
                    "env": "CFGPIPE_CP1_HOST",
                    "arg": "host",
                },
                "port": {
                    "type": "integer",
                    "default": "3000",
                    "env": "CFGPIPE_CP1_PORT",
                    "file": str(value_file),
                    "arg": "port",
                },
            },
        )
    
        result = run_cfgpipe(
            entrypoint_argv,
            schema_path=schema_path,

                "CFGPIPE_CP1_PORT": "5000",
            },
            arg_candidates=["--host=arg-host", "-port=7000"],

        )

        ],
    )
    def test_primary_store_resolves(
        entrypoint_argv: list[str],
        tmp_path: Path,
        store_server,
        store_key: str,
        param_key: str,
        param_type: str,
        value: str,
        version: int,
        default: str | None,
    ) -> None:

        field: dict[str, object] = {"type": param_type, "primary-store": store_key}

            field["default"] = default

            schema_path=schema_path,

        )

.evaluation_tests/utils.py:216: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701da0a810d0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

/usr/local/lib/python3.12/queue.py:179: Empty

.evaluation_tests/utils.py:216: 
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9f39dfa0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9dac7c20>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9dd948c0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

        schema_path = _write_schema(
            tmp_path,

        )

>       assert_success(result)

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9d7602c0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701da06f5070>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9de8e1b0>, block = True, timeout = 3.0

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9dca02c0>, block = True
timeout = 2.9999993797391653

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty

self = <queue.Queue object at 0x701d9f392b40>, block = True
timeout = 2.9999993704259396

    def get(self, block=True, timeout=None):
        '''Remove and return an item from the queue.
    
        If optional args 'block' is true and 'timeout' is None (the default),
        block if necessary until an item is available. If 'timeout' is
        a non-negative number, it blocks at most 'timeout' seconds and raises
        the Empty exception if no item was available within that time.
        Otherwise ('block' is false), return an item if one is immediately
        available, else raise the Empty exception ('timeout' is ignored
        in that case).
        '''
        with self.not_empty:
            if not block:
                if not self._qsize():
                    raise Empty
            elif timeout is None:
                while not self._qsize():
                    self.not_empty.wait()
            elif timeout < 0:
                raise ValueError("'timeout' must be a non-negative number")
            else:
                endtime = time() + timeout
                while not self._qsize():
                    remaining = endtime - time()
                    if remaining <= 0.0:
>                       raise Empty
E                       _queue.Empty
